Typed[any]\\n187: \\n188: type Typed[t comparable] struct {\\n189: \\t// queue defines the order in which we will work on items. Every\\n190: \\t// element of queue should be in the dirty set and not in the\\n191: \\t// processing set.\\n192: \\tqueue Queue[t]\\n193: \\n194: \\t// dirty defines all of the items that need to be processed.\\n195: \\tdirty set[t]\\n196: \\n197: \\t// Things that are currently being processed are in the processing set.\\n198: \\t// These things may be simultaneously in the dirty set. When we finish\\n199: \\t// processing something and remove it from this set, we'll check if\\n200: \\t// it's in the dirty set, and if so, add it to the queue.\\n201: \\tprocessing set[t]\\n202: \\n203: \\tcond *sync.Cond\\n204: \\n205: \\tshuttingDown bool\\n206: \\tdrain        bool\\n207: \\n208: \\tmetrics queueMetrics[t]\\n209: \\n210: \\tunfinishedWorkUpdatePeriod time.Duration\\n211: \\tclock                      clock.WithTicker\\n212: }\\n213: \\n214: type empty struct{}\\n215: type set[t comparable] map[t]empty\\n216: \\n217: func (s set[t]) has(item t) bool {\\n218: \\t_, exists := s[item]\\n219: \\treturn exists\\n220: }\\n221: \\n222: func (s set[t]) insert(item t) {\\n223: \\ts[item] = empty{}\\n224: }\\n225: \\n226: func (s set[t]) delete(item t) {\\n227: \\tdelete(s, item)\\n228: }\\n229: \\n230: func (s set[t]) len() int {\\n231: \\treturn len(s)\\n232: }\\n233: \\n234: // Add marks item as needing processing.\\n235: func (q *Typed[T]) Add(item T) {\\n236: \\tq.cond.L.Lock()\\n237: \\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\\n238: \\tif q.shuttingDown {\\n239: \\t\\treturn\\n240: \\t}\\n241: \\tif q.dirty.has(item) {\\n242: \\t\\t// the same item is added again before it is processed, call the Touch\\n243: \\t\\t// function if the queue cares about it (for e.g, reset its priority)\\n244: \\t\\tif !q.processing.has(item) {\\n245: \\t\\t\\tq.queue.Touch(item)\\n246: \\t\\t}\\n247: \\t\\treturn\\n248: \\t}\\n249: \\n250: \\tq.metrics.add(item)\\n251: \\n252: \\tq.dirty.insert(item)\\n253: \\tif q.processing.has(item) {\\n254: \\t\\treturn\\n255: \\t}\\n256: \\n257: \\tq.queue.Push(item)\\n258: \\tq.cond.Signal()\\n259: }\\n260: \\n261: // Len returns the current queue length, for informational purposes only. You\\n262: // shouldn't e.g. gate a call to Add() or Get() on Len() being a particular\\n263: // value, that can't be synchronized properly.\\n264: func (q *Typed[T]) Len() int {\\n265: \\tq.cond.L.Lock()\\n266: \\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\\n267: \\treturn q.queue.Len()\\n268: }\\n269: \\n270: // Get blocks until it can return an item to be processed. If shutdown = true,\\n271: // the caller should end their goroutine. You must call Done with item when you\\n272: // have finished processing it.\\n273: func (q *Typed[T]) Get() (item T, shutdown bool) {\\n274: \\tq.cond.L.Lock()\\n275: \\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\\n276: \\tfor q.queue.Len() == 0 && !q.shuttingDown {\\n277: \\t\\tq.cond.Wait()\\n278: \\t}\\n279: \\tif q.queue.Len() == 0 {\\n280: \\t\\t// We must be shutting down.\\n281: \\t\\treturn *new(T), true\\n282: \\t}\\n283: \\n284: \\titem = q.queue.Pop()\\n285: \\n286: \\tq.metrics.get(item)\\n287: \\n288: \\tq.processing.insert(item)\\n289: \\tq.dirty.delete(item)\\n290: \\n291: \\treturn item, false\\n292: }\\n293: \\n294: // Done marks item as done processing, and if it has been marked as dirty again\\n295: // while it was being processed, it will be re-added to the queue for\\n296: // re-processing.\\n297: func (q *Typed[T]) Done(item T) {\\n298: \\tq.cond.L.Lock()\\n299: \\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\\n300: \\n301: \\tq.metrics.done(item)\\n302: \\n303: \\tq.processing.delete(item)\\n304: \\tif q.dirty.has(item) {\\n305: \\t\\tq.queue.Push(item)\\n306: \\t\\tq.cond.Signal()\\n307: \\t} else if q.processing.len() == 0 {\\n308: \\t\\tq.cond.Signal()\\n309: \\t}\\n310: }\\n311: \\n312: // ShutDown will cause q to ignore all new items added to it and\\n313: // immediately instruct the worker goroutines to exit.\\n314: func (q *Typed[T]) ShutDown() {\\n315: \\tq.cond.L.Lock()\\n316: \\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\\n317: \\n318: \\tq.drain = false\\n319: \\tq.shuttingDown = true\\n320: \\tq.cond.Broadcast()\\n321: }\\n322: \\n323: // ShutDownWithDrain will cause q to ignore all new items added to it. As soon\\n324: // as the worker goroutines have \\\"drained\\\", i.e: finished processing and called\\n325: // Done on all existing items in the queue; they will be instructed to exit and\\n326: // ShutDownWithDrain will return. Hence: a strict requirement for using this is;\\n327: // your workers must ensure that Done is called on all items in the queue once\\n328: // the shut down has been initiated, if that is not the case: this will block\\n329: // indefinitely. It is, however, safe to call ShutDown after having called\\n330: // ShutDownWithDrain, as to force the queue shut down to terminate immediately\\n331: // without waiting for the drainage.\\n332: func As soon\n324: // as the worker goroutines have \"drained\", i.e: finished processing and called\n325: // Done on all existing items in the queue; they will be instructed to exit and\n326: // ShutDownWithDrain will return. Hence: a strict requirement for using this is;\n327: // your workers must ensure that Done is called on all items in the queue once\n328: // the shut down has been initiated, if that is not the case: this will block\n329: // indefinitely. It is, however, safe to call ShutDown after having called\n330: // ShutDownWithDrain, as to force the queue shut down to terminate immediately\n331: // without waiting for the drainage.\n332: func (q *Typed[T]) ShutDownWithDrain() {\n333: \tq.cond.L.Lock()\n334: \tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n335: \n336: \tq.drain = true\n337: \tq.shuttingDown = true\n338: \tq.cond.Broadcast()\n339: \n340: \tfor q.processing.len() != 0 && q.drain {\n341: \t\tq.cond.Wait()\n342: \t}\n343: }\n344: \n345: func (q *Typed[T]) ShuttingDown() bool {\n346: \tq.cond.L.Lock()\n347: \tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n348: \n349: \treturn q.shuttingDown\n350: }\n351: \n352: func (q *Typed[T]) updateUnfinishedWorkLoop() {\n353: \tt := q.clock.NewTicker(q.unfinishedWorkUpdatePeriod)\n354: \tdefer t.Stop()\n355: \tfor range t.C() {\n356: \t\tif !func() bool {\n357: \t\t\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n358: \t\t\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n359: \t\t\tif !q.shuttingDown {\n360: \t\t\t\tq.metrics.updateUnfinishedWork()\n361: \t\t\t\treturn true\n362: \t\t\t}\n363: \t\t\treturn false\n364: \n365: \t\t}() {\n366: \t\t\treturn\n367: \t\t}\n368: \t}\n369: }\n370: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0@d17b464c6fcd3273e4b1f695890bf0af7d5b272d/-/blob/staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/queue.go"}}}

through a comprehensive pattern located in staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/. The Typed[T] struct manages a queue of items with dirty and processing sets to handle re-queueing. Add marks items for processing, Get retrieves and marks items as processing, and Done marks completion and re-adds if item was marked dirty again.\\n\\n5. **Controller Reconcile Loop Pattern**: Implemented across numerous controllers including staging/src/k8s.io/sample-controller/controller.go, pkg/controller/job/job_controller.go, pkg/controller/replicaset/replica_set.go, pkg/controller/bootstrap/tokencleaner.go, pkg/controller/serviceaccount/serviceaccounts_controller.go, pkg/controller/volume/pvcprotection/pvc_protection_controller.go, and staging/src/k8s.io/cloud-provider/controllers/node/node_controller.go. The pattern follows: (1) Run() starts multiple workers, (2) runWorker() continuously calls processNextWorkItem(), (3) processNextWorkItem() calls queue.Get(), executes syncHandler()/sync logic, calls queue.Done(), and on error calls queue.AddRateLimited() for retry with backoff.\\n\\nThe typical usage creates a rate limiter combining ItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter and BucketRateLimiter via NewTypedMaxOfRateLimiter (e.g., in sample-controller line 110-113), creates a RateLimitingInterface queue with NewTypedRateLimitingQueue, and uses a worker pattern that repeatedly calls queue.Get() to retrieve items, process them (the reconcile logic), and calls queue.Done() to mark completion.
